SELECT "s0"."Id", "s0"."AlbumId", "s0"."Duration", "s0"."Genre", "s0"."ReleaseDate", "s0"."Title", "a"."Id", "a"."ArtistId", "a"."Genre", "a"."ReleaseYear", "a"."Title", "a0"."Id", "a0"."Genre", "a0"."Name"
FROM (
    SELECT "s"."Id", "s"."AlbumId", "s"."Duration", "s"."Genre", "s"."ReleaseDate", "s"."Title"
    FROM "Songs" AS "s"
    ORDER BY "s"."Title"
    LIMIT @__p_1 OFFSET @__p_0
) AS "s0"
INNER JOIN "Albums" AS "a" ON "s0"."AlbumId" = "a"."Id"
INNER JOIN "Artists" AS "a0" ON "a"."ArtistId" = "a0"."Id"
ORDER BY "s0"."Title"
